> Per-property experiments (property midpoint reference, no rule cap)

**Model file:** `ACASXU_run2a_4_8_batch_2000.onnx`

**Experiment types:** full_rule, per_layer, impl_ablation

## How To Read Counts

- Each `Y/N/T/o` row is one verification query: `(property, Оө, true_class, target_label != true_class, rule)`.
- Self-target rows (`target_label == true_class`) are stored as `-` in the CSVs and are excluded from every denominator.
- Denominators in the summary tables count valid queries, not properties, models, or experiment directories.
- For the end-to-end pipeline and a worked example of counts such as `8/40`, see [`COUNTS_AND_PIPELINE.md`](COUNTS_AND_PIPELINE.md).

**Per-model query accounting (the source of denominators such as `8/40`)**

| Property | True class(es) | Valid queries per Оө | Formula |
|----------|----------------|---------------------|---------|
| prop1 | 0, 1 | 8 | 2 true classes Г— 4 non-self targets |
| prop2 | 0, 1 | 8 | 2 true classes Г— 4 non-self targets |
| prop3 | 1 | 4 | 1 true classes Г— 4 non-self targets |
| prop4 | 1 | 4 | 1 true classes Г— 4 non-self targets |
| **Total** | вҖ“ | **24** | **8 + 8 + 4 + 4** |

#### Per-Layer

_Shared unary/baseline tables are shown once below using deduplicated query rows. Layer-specific implication tables remain grouped by layer pair._
